the transactionManager is in error states.\\n272:                     forceClose = true;\\n273:                 }\\n274:             }\\n275:             try {\\n276:                 runOnce();\\n277:             } catch (Exception e) {\\n278:                 log.error(\\\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \\\", e);\\n279:             }\\n280:         }\\n281: \\n282:         if (forceClose) {\\n283:             // We need to fail all the incomplete transactional requests and batches and wake up the threads waiting on\\n284:             // the futures.\\n285:             if (transactionManager != null) {\\n286:                 log.debug(\\\"Aborting incomplete transactional requests due to forced shutdown\\\");\\n287:                 transactionManager.close();\\n288:             }\\n289:             log.debug(\\\"Aborting incomplete batches due to forced shutdown\\\");\\n290:             this.accumulator.abortIncompleteBatches();\\n291:         }\\n292:         try {\\n293:             this.client.close();\\n294:         } catch (Exception e) {\\n295:             log.error(\\\"Failed to close network client\\\", e);\\n296:         }\\n297: \\n298:         log.debug(\\\"Shutdown of Kafka producer I/O thread has completed.\\\");\\n299:     }\\n300: \\n301:     /**\\n302:      * Run a single iteration of sending\\n303:      *\\n304:      */\\n305:     void runOnce() {\\n306:         if (transactionManager != null) {\\n307:             try {\\n308:                 transactionManager.maybeResolveSequences();\\n309: \\n310:                 RuntimeException lastError = transactionManager.lastError();\\n311: \\n312:                 // do not continue sending if the transaction manager is in a failed state\\n313:                 if (transactionManager.hasFatalError()) {\\n314:                     if (lastError != null)\\n315:                         maybeAbortBatches(lastError);\\n316:                     client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n317:                     return;\\n318:                 }\\n319: \\n320:                 if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError() && shouldHandleAuthorizationError(lastError)) {\\n321:                     return;\\n322:                 }\\n323: \\n324:                 // Check whether we need a new producerId. If so, we will enqueue an InitProducerId\\n325:                 // request which will be sent below\\n326:                 transactionManager.bumpIdempotentEpochAndResetIdIfNeeded();\\n327: \\n328:                 if (maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest()) {\\n329:                     return;\\n330:                 }\\n331:             } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\\n332:                 // This is already logged as error, but propagated here to perform any clean ups.\\n333:                 log.trace(\\\"Authentication exception while processing transactional request\\\", e);\\n334:                 transactionManager.authenticationFailed(e);\\n335:             }\\n336:         }\\n337: \\n338:         long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\\n339:         long pollTimeout = sendProducerData(currentTimeMs);\\n340:         client.poll(pollTimeout, currentTimeMs);\\n341:     }\\n342: \\n343:     // We handle {@code TransactionalIdAuthorizationException} and {@code ClusterAuthorizationException} by first\\n344:     // failing the inflight requests, then transition the state to UNINITIALIZED so that the user doesn't need to\\n345:     // instantiate the producer again.\\n346:     private boolean shouldHandleAuthorizationError(RuntimeException exception) {\\n347:         if (exception instanceof TransactionalIdAuthorizationException ||\\n348:                         exception instanceof ClusterAuthorizationException) {\\n349:             transactionManager.failPendingRequests(new AuthenticationException(exception));\\n350:             maybeAbortBatches(exception);\\n351:             transactionManager.transitionToUninitialized(exception);\\n352:             return true;\\n353:         }\\n354:         return false;\\n355:     }\\n356: \\n357:     private long sendProducerData(long now) {\\n358:         MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot = metadata.fetchMetadataSnapshot();\\n359:         // get the list of partitions with data ready to send\\n360:         RecordAccumulator.ReadyCheckResult result = this.accumulator.ready(metadataSnapshot, now);\\n361: \\n362:         // if there are any partitions whose leaders are not known yet, force metadata update\\n363:         if (!result.unknownLeaderTopics.isEmpty()) {\\n364:             // The set of topics with unknown leader contains topics with leader election pending as well as\\n365:             // topics which may have expired. Add the topic again to metadata to ensure it is included\\n366:             // and request metadata update, since there are messages to send to the topic.\\n367:             for (String topic : result.unknownLeaderTopics)\\n368:                 this.metadata.add(topic, now);\\n369: \\n370:             log.debug(\\\"Requesting metadata update due to unknown leader topics from the batched records: {}\\\",\\n371:                 result.unknownLeaderTopics);\\n372:             this.metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n373:         }\\n374: \\n375:         // remove any nodes we aren't ready to send to\\n376:         Iterator<Node> iter = result.readyNodes.iterator();\\n377:         long notReadyTimeout = Long.MAX_VALUE;\\n378:         while (iter.hasNext()) {\\n379:             Node node = iter.next();\\n380:             if (!this.client.ready(node, now)) {\\n381:                 // Update just the readyTimeMs of the latency stats, so that it moves forward\\n382:                 // every time the batch is ready (then the difference between readyTimeMs and\\n383:                 // drainTimeMs would represent how long data is waiting for the node).\\n384:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, false);\\n385:                 iter.remove();\\n386:                 notReadyTimeout = Math.min(notReadyTimeout, this.client.pollDelayMs(node, now));\\n387:             } else {\\n388:                 // Update both readyTimeMs and drainTimeMs, this would \\\"reset\\\" the node\\n389:                 // latency.\\n390:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, true);\\n391:             }\\n392:         }\\n393: \\n394:         // create produce requests\\n395:         Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches = this.accumulator.drain(metadataSnapshot, result.readyNodes, this.maxRequestSize, now);\\n396:         addToInflightBatches(batches);\\n397:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder) {\\n398:             // Mute all the partitions drained\\n399:             for (List<ProducerBatch> batchList : batches.values()) {\\n400:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batchList)\\n401:                     this.accumulator.mutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\\n402:             }\\n403:         }\\n404: \\n405:         accumulator.resetNextBatchExpiryTime();\\n406:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);\\n407:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);\\n408:         expiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\\n409: \\n410:         // Reset the producer id if an expired batch has previously been sent to the broker. Also update the metrics\\n411:         // for expired batches. see the documentation of @TransactionState.resetIdempotentProducerId to understand why\\n412:         // we need to reset the producer id here.\\n413:         if (!expiredBatches.isEmpty())\\n414:             log.trace(\\\"Expired {} batches in accumulator\\\", expiredBatches.size());\\n415:         for (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\\n416:             String errorMessage = \\\"Expiring \\\" + expiredBatch.recordCount + \\\" record(s) for \\\" + expiredBatch.topicPartition\\n417:                 + \\\":\\\" + (now - expiredBatch.createdMs) + \\\" ms has passed since batch creation\\\";\\n418:             failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\\n419:             if (transactionManager != null && expiredBatch.inRetry()) {\\n420:                 // This ensures that no new batches are drained until the current in flight batches are fully resolved.\\n421:                 transactionManager.markSequenceUnresolved(expiredBatch);\\n422:             }\\n423:         }\\n424:         sensors.updateProduceRequestMetrics(batches);\\n425: \\n426:         // If we have any nodes that are ready to send + have sendable data, poll with 0 timeout so this can immediately\\n427:         // loop and try sending more data. Otherwise, the timeout will be the smaller value between next batch expiry\\n428:         // time, and the delay time for checking data availability. Note that the nodes may have data that isn't yet\\n429:         // sendable due to lingering, backing off, etc. This specifically does not include nodes with sendable data\\n430:         // that aren't ready to send since they would cause busy looping.\\n431:         long pollTimeout = Math.min(result.nextReadyCheckDelayMs, notReadyTimeout);\\n432:         pollTimeout = Math.min(pollTimeout, this.accumulator.nextExpiryTimeMs() - now);\\n433:         pollTimeout = Math.max(pollTimeout, 0);\\n434:         if (!result.readyNodes.isEmpty()) {\\n435:             log.trace(\\\"Nodes with data ready to send: {}\\\", result.readyNodes);\\n436:             // if some partitions are already ready to be sent, the select time would be 0;\\n437:             // otherwise if some partition already has some data accumulated but not ready yet,\\n438:             // the select time will be the time difference between now and its linger expiry time;\\n439:             // otherwise the select time will be the time difference between now and the metadata expiry time;\\n440:             pollTimeout = 0;\\n441:         }\\n442:         sendProduceRequests(batches, now);\\n443:         return pollTimeout;\\n444:     }\\n445: \\n446:     /**\\n447:      * Returns true if a transactional request is sent or polled, or if a FindCoordinator request is enqueued\\n448:      */\\n449:     private boolean maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest() {\\n450:         if (transactionManager.hasInFlightRequest()) {\\n451:             // as long as there are outstanding transactional requests, we simply wait for them to return\\n452:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n453:             return true;\\n454:         }\\n455: \\n456:         if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError()) {\\n457:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(transactionManager.lastError());\\n458:         } else if (transactionManager.isAborting()) {\\n459:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(new TransactionAbortedException());\\n460:         }\\n461: \\n462:         TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler = transactionManager.nextRequest(accumulator.hasIncomplete());\\n463:         if (nextRequestHandler == null)\\n464:             return false;\\n465: \\n466:         AbstractRequest.Builder<?> requestBuilder = nextRequestHandler.requestBuilder();\\n467:         Node targetNode = null;\\n468:         try {\\n469:             FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType = nextRequestHandler.coordinatorType();\\n470:             targetNode = coordinatorType != null ?\\n471:                     transactionManager.coordinator(coordinatorType) :\\n472:                     client.leastLoadedNode(time.milliseconds()).node();\\n473:             if (targetNode != null) {\\n474:                 if (!awaitNodeReady(targetNode, coordinatorType)) {\\n475:                     log.trace(\\\"Target node {} not ready within request timeout, will retry when node is ready.\\\", targetNode);\\n476:                     maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\\n477:                     return true;\\n478:                 }\\n479:             } else if (coordinatorType != null) {\\n480:                 log.trace(\\\"Coordinator not known for {}, will retry {} after finding coordinator.\\\", coordinatorType, requestBuilder.apiKey());\\n481:                 maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\\n482:                 return true;\\n483:             } else {\\n484:                 log.trace(\\\"No nodes available to send requests, will poll and retry when until a node is ready.\\\");\\n485:                 transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\\n486:                 client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n487:                 return true;\\n488:             }\\n489: \\n490:             if (nextRequestHandler.isRetry())\\n491:                 time.sleep(nextRequestHandler.retryBackoffMs());\\n492: \\n493:             long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\\n494:             ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(targetNode.idString(), requestBuilder, currentTimeMs,\\n495:                 true, requestTimeoutMs, nextRequestHandler);\\n496:             log.debug(\\\"Sending transactional request {} to node {} with correlation ID {}\\\", requestBuilder, targetNode, clientRequest.correlationId());\\n497:             client.send(clientRequest, currentTimeMs);\\n498:             transactionManager.setInFlightCorrelationId(clientRequest.correlationId());\\n499:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\\n500:             return true;\\n501:         } catch (IOException e) {\\n502:             log.debug(\\\"Disconnect from {} while trying to send request {}. Going \\\" +\\n503:                     \\\"to back off and retry.\\\", targetNode, requestBuilder, e);\\n504:             // We break here so that we pick up the FindCoordinator request immediately.\\n505:             maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\\n506:             return true;\\n507:         }\\n508:     }\\n509: \\n510:     private void maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler) {\\n511:         if (nextRequestHandler.needsCoordinator()) {\\n512:             transactionManager.lookupCoordinator(nextRequestHandler);\\n513:         } else {\\n514:             // For non-coordinator requests, sleep here to prevent a tight loop when no node is available\\n515:             time.sleep(retryBackoffMs);\\n516:             metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n517:         }\\n518: \\n519:         transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\\n520:     }\\n521: \\n522:     private void maybeAbortBatches(RuntimeException exception) {\\n523:         if (accumulator.hasIncomplete()) {\\n524:             log.error(\\\"Aborting producer batches due to fatal error\\\", exception);\\n525:             accumulator.abortBatches(exception);\\n526:         }\\n527:     }\\n528: \\n529:     /**\\n530:      * Start closing the sender (won't actually complete until all data is sent out)\\n531:      */\\n532:     public void initiateClose() {\\n533:         // Ensure accumulator is closed first to guarantee that no more appends are accepted after\\n534:         // breaking from the sender loop. Otherwise, we may miss some callbacks when shutting down.\\n535:         this.accumulator.close();\\n536:         this.running = false;\\n537:         this.wakeup();\\n538:     }\\n539: \\n540:     /**\\n541:      * Closes the sender without sending out any pending messages.\\n542:      */\\n543:     public void forceClose() {\\n544:         this.forceClose = true;\\n545:         initiateClose();\\n546:     }\\n547: \\n548:     public boolean isRunning() {\\n549:         return running;\\n550:     }\\n551: \\n552:     private boolean awaitNodeReady(Node node, FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType) throws IOException {\\n553:         if (NetworkClientUtils.awaitReady(client, node, time, requestTimeoutMs)) {\\n554:             if (coordinatorType == FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType.TRANSACTION) {\\n555:                 // Indicate to the transaction manager that the coordinator is ready, allowing it to check ApiVersions\\n556:                 // This allows us to bump transactional epochs even if the coordinator is temporarily unavailable at\\n557:                 // the time when the abortable error is handled\\n558:                 transactionManager.handleCoordinatorReady();\\n559:             }\\n560:             return true;\\n561:         }\\n562:         return false;\\n563:     }\\n564: \\n565:     /**\\n566:      * Handle a produce response\\n567:      */\\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames, long now) {\\n569:         RequestHeader requestHeader = response.requestHeader();\\n570:         int correlationId = requestHeader.correlationId();\\n571:         if (response.wasTimedOut()) {\\n572:             log.trace(\\\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\\\",\\n573:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\\n574:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n575:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.REQUEST_TIMED_OUT, String.format(\\\"Disconnected from node %s due to timeout\\\", response.destination())),\\n576:                         correlationId, now, null);\\n577:         } else if (response.wasDisconnected()) {\\n578:             log.trace(\\\"Cancelled request with header {} due to node {} being disconnected\\\",\\n579:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\\n580:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n581:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NETWORK_EXCEPTION, String.format(\\\"Disconnected from node %s\\\", response.destination())),\\n582:                         correlationId, now, null);\\n583:         } else if (response.versionMismatch() != null) {\\n584:             log.warn(\\\"Cancelled request {} due to a version mismatch with node {}\\\",\\n585:                     response, response.destination(), response.versionMismatch());\\n586:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n587:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION), correlationId, now, null);\\n588:         } else {\\n589:             log.trace(\\\"Received produce response from node {} with correlation id {}\\\", response.destination(), correlationId);\\n590:             // if we have a response, parse it\\n591:             if (response.hasResponse()) {\\n592:                 // Sender should exercise PartitionProduceResponse rather than ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse\\n593:                 // https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-10696\\n594:                 ProduceResponse produceResponse = (ProduceResponse) response.responseBody();\\n595:                 // This will be set by completeBatch.\\n596:                 Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo = new HashMap<>();\\n597:                 produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\\n598:                     ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\\n600:                             p.baseOffset(),\\n601:                             p.logAppendTimeMs(),\\n602:                             p.logStartOffset(),\\n603:                             p.recordErrors()\\n604:                                 .stream()\\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\\n606:                                 .collect(Collectors.toList()),\\n607:                             p.errorMessage(),\\n608:                             p.currentLeader());\\n609: \\n610:                     // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\\n611:                     // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\\n612:                     // topic name in the response will be empty.\\n613:                     // For older versions, topic id is zero, and we will find the batch based on the topic name.\\n614:                     TopicPartition tp = (!r.topicId().equals(Uuid.ZERO_UUID) && topicNames.containsKey(r.topicId())) ?\\n615:                             new TopicPartition(topicNames.get(r.topicId()), p.index()) :\\n616:                             new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\\n617: \\n618:                     ProducerBatch batch = batches.get(tp);\\n619:                     if (batch == null) {\\n620:                         throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"Can't find batch created for topic id \\\" + r.topicId() +\\n621:                                 \\\" topic name \\\" + r.name() + \\\" partition \\\" + p.index() + \\\" using \\\" + topicNames);\\n622:                     }\\n623:                     completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\\n624:                 }));\\n625: \\n626:                 if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\\n630:                         .collect(\\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\\n633:                     if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\\n634:                         updatedPartitions.forEach(\\n635:                             part -> log.debug(\\\"For {} leader was updated.\\\", part)\\n636:                         );\\n637:                     }\\n638:                 }\\n639: \\n640:                 this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\\n641:             } else {\\n642:                 // this is the acks = 0 case, just complete all requests\\n643:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values()) {\\n644:                     completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NONE), correlationId, now, null);\\n645:                 }\\n646:             }\\n647:         }\\n648:     }\\n649: \\n650:     /**\\n651:      * Complete or retry the given batch of records.\\n652:      *\\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\\n654:      * @param response The produce response\\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\\n658:      */\\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\\n662: \\n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\\n667:             log.warn(\\n668:                 \\\"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n669:                 correlationId,\\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\\n680:                 log.warn(\\n681:                     \\\"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n682:                     correlationId,\\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\\n691:                 //\\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\\n694:             } else {\\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\\n699:             }\\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\\n702:                     log.warn(\\\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \\\" +\\n703:                             \\\"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\\\",\\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\\n705:                 } else {\\n706:                     log.warn(\\\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \\\" +\\n707:                             \\\"to request metadata update now\\\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\\n708:                 }\\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\\n710:                     log.debug(\\\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\\\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\\n715:                     }\\n716:                 }\\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n718:             }\\n719:         } else {\\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\\n721:         }\\n722: \\n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\\n726:     }\\n727: \\n728:     /**\\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\\n730:      * e.g \\\"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\\\"\\n731:      */\\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\\n734:                 \\\"\\\" : String.format(\\\". Error Message: %s\\\", response.errorMessage);\\n735:         return String.format(\\\"%s%s\\\", response.error, errorMessageSuffix);\\n736:     }\\n737: \\n738:     private void reenqueueBatch(ProducerBatch batch, long currentTimeMs) {\\n739:         this.accumulator.reenqueue(batch, currentTimeMs);\\n740:         maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\\n741:         this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n742:     }\\n743: \\n744:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n745:         if (transactionManager != null) {\\n746:             transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\\n747:         }\\n748: \\n749:         if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\\n750:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n751:         }\\n752:     }\\n753: \\n754:     private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\\n755:                            ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\\n756:                            boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\\n757:         final RuntimeException topLevelException;\\n758:         if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n759:             topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\\n760:         else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n761:             topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\\\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\\\");\\n762:         else\\n763:             topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\\n764: \\n765:         if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\\n766:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n767:         } else {\\n768:             Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\\n769:             for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\\n770:                 // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\\n771:                 // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\\n772:                 // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\\n773:                 // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\\n776:                     errorMessage = recordError.message;\\n777:                 } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\\n778:                     errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\\n779:                 } else {\\n780:                     errorMessage = response.error.message();\\n781:                 }\\n782: \\n783:                 // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\\n784:                 // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\\n785:                 if RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\\n793:                 RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\\n794:                 if (exception != null) {\\n795:                     return exception;\\n796:                 } else {\\n797:                     // If the response contains record errors, then the records which failed validation\\n798:                     // will be present in the response. To avoid confusion for the remaining records, we\\n799:                     // return a generic exception.\\n800:                     return new KafkaException(\\\"Failed to append record because it was part of a batch \\\" +\\n801:                         \\\"which had one more more invalid records\\\");\\n802:                 }\\n803:             };\\n804: \\n805:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, recordExceptions, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n806:         }\\n807:     }\\n808: \\n809:     private void failBatch(\\n810:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n811:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n812:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n813:     ) {\\n814:         failBatch(batch, topLevelException, batchIndex -> topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n815:     }\\n816: \\n817:     private void failBatch(\\n818:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n819:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n820:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\\n821:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n822:     ) {\\n823:         this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n824: \\n825:         if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\\n826:             if (transactionManager != null) {\\n827:                 try {\\n828:                     // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\\n829:                     // attempted.          maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n836:         }\\n837:     }\\n838: \\n839:     /**\\n840:      * We can retry a send if the error is transient and the number of attempts taken is fewer than the maximum allowed.\\n841:      * We can also retry OutOfOrderSequence exceptions for future batches, since if the first batch has failed, the\\n842:      * future batches are certain to fail with an OutOfOrderSequence exception.\\n843:      */\\n844:     private boolean canRetry(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long now) {\\n845:         return (transactionManager == null ?\\n849:                     response.error.exception() instanceof RetriableException :\\n850:                     transactionManager.canRetry(response, batch));\\n851:     }\\n852: \\n853:     /**\\n854:      * Transfer the record batches into a list of produce requests on a per-node basis\\n855:      */\\n856:     private void sendProduceRequests(Map<Integer, Sender.sendProducerData, before client.poll.\n193:                         // The !batch.isDone() invariant should always hold. An IllegalStateException\n194:                         // exception will be thrown if the invariant is violated.\n195:                         if (!batch.isDone()) {\n196:                             expiredBatches.add(batch);\n197:                         } else {\n198:                             throw new IllegalStateException(batch.topicPartition + \" batch created at \" +\n199:                                 batch.createdMs + \" gets unexpected final state \" + batch.finalState());\n200:                         }\n201:                     } else {\n202:                         accumulator.maybeUpdateNextBatchExpiryTime(batch);\n203:                         break;\n204:                     }\n205:                 }\n206:                 if (partitionInFlightBatches.isEmpty()) {\n207:                     batchIt.remove();\n208:                 }\n209:             }\n210:         }\n211:         return expiredBatches;\n212:     }\n213: \n214:     private void addToInflightBatches(List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\n215:         for (ProducerBatch batch : batches) {\n216:             List<ProducerBatch> inflightBatchList = inFlightBatches.computeIfAbsent(batch.topicPartition,\n217:                 k -> new ArrayList<>());\n218:             inflightBatchList.add(batch);\n219:         }\n220:     }\n221: \n222:     public void addToInflightBatches(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches) {\n223:         for (List<ProducerBatch> batchList : batches.values()) {\n224:             addToInflightBatches(batchList);\n225:         }\n226:     }\n227: \n228:     private boolean hasPendingTransactionalRequests() {\n229:         return transactionManager != null && transactionManager.hasPendingRequests() && transactionManager.hasOngoingTransaction();\n230:     }\n231: \n232:     /**\n233:      * The main run loop for the sender thread\n234:      */\n235:     @Override\n236:     public void run() {\n237:         log.debug(\"Starting Kafka producer I/O thread.\");\n238: \n239:         // main loop, runs until close is called\n240:         while (running) {\n241:             try {\n242:                 runOnce();\n243:             } catch (Exception e) {\n244:                 log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n245:             }\n246:         }\n247: \n248:         log.debug(\"Beginning shutdown of Kafka producer I/O thread, sending remaining records.\");\n249: \n250:         // okay we stopped accepting requests but there may still be\n251:         // requests in the transaction manager, accumulator or waiting for acknowledgment,\n252:         // wait until these are completed.\n253:         while (!forceClose && ((this.accumulator.hasUndrained() || this.client.inFlightRequestCount() > 0) || hasPendingTransactionalRequests())) {\n254:             try {\n255:                 runOnce();\n256:             } catch (Exception e) {\n257:                 log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n258:             }\n259:         }\n260: \n261:         // Abort the transaction if any commit or abort didn't go through the transaction manager's queue\n262:         while (!forceClose && transactionManager != null && transactionManager.hasOngoingTransaction()) {\n263:             if (!transactionManager.isCompleting()) {\n264:                 log.info(\"Aborting incomplete transaction due to shutdown\");\n265:                 try {\n266:                     // It is possible for the transaction manager to throw errors when aborting. Catch these\n267:                     // so as not to interfere with the rest of the shutdown logic.\n268:                     transactionManager.beginAbort();\n269:                 } catch (Exception e) {\n270:                     log.error(\"Error in kafka producer I/O thread while aborting transaction when during closing: \", e);\n271:                     // Force close in case the transactionManager is in error states.\n272:                     forceClose = true;\n273:                 }\n274:             }\n275:             try {\n276:                 runOnce();\n277:             } catch (Exception e) {\n278:                 log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n279:             }\n280:         }\n281: \n282:         if (forceClose) {\n283:             // We need to fail all the incomplete transactional requests and batches and wake up the threads waiting on\n284:             // the futures.\n285:             if (transactionManager != null) {\n286:                 log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete transactional requests due to forced shutdown\");\n287:                 transactionManager.close();\n288:             }\n289:             log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete batches due to forced shutdown\");\n290:             this.accumulator.abortIncompleteBatches();\n291:         }\n292:         try {\n293:             this.client.close();\n294:         } catch (Exception e) {\n295:             log.error(\"Failed to close network client\", e);\n296:         }\n297: \n298:         log.debug(\"Shutdown of Kafka producer I/O thread has completed.\");\n299:     }\n300: \n301:     /**\n302:      * Run a single iteration of sending\n303:      *\n304:      */\n305:     void runOnce() {\n306:         if (transactionManager != null) {\n307:             try {\n308:                 transactionManager.maybeResolveSequences();\n309: \n310:                 RuntimeException lastError = transactionManager.lastError();\n311: \n312:                 // do not continue sending if the transaction manager is in a failed state\n313:                 if (transactionManager.hasFatalError()) {\n314:                     if (lastError != null)\n315:                         maybeAbortBatches(lastError);\n316:                     client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n317:                     return;\n318:                 }\n319: \n320:                 if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError() && shouldHandleAuthorizationError(lastError)) {\n321:                     return;\n322:                 }\n323: \n324:                 // Check whether we need a new producerId. If so, we will enqueue an InitProducerId\n325:                 // request which will be sent below\n326:                 transactionManager.bumpIdempotentEpochAndResetIdIfNeeded();\n327: \n328:                 if (maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest()) {\n329:                     return;\n330:                 }\n331:             } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n332:                 // This is already logged as error, but propagated here to perform any clean ups.\n333:                 log.trace(\"Authentication exception while processing transactional request\", e);\n334:                 transactionManager.authenticationFailed(e);\n335:             }\n336:         }\n337: \n338:         long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n339:         long pollTimeout = sendProducerData(currentTimeMs);\n340:         client.poll(pollTimeout, currentTimeMs);\n341:     }\n342: \n343:     // We handle {@code TransactionalIdAuthorizationException} and {@code ClusterAuthorizationException} by first\n344:     // failing the inflight requests, then transition the state to UNINITIALIZED so that the user doesn't need to\n345:     // instantiate the producer again.\n346:     private boolean shouldHandleAuthorizationError(RuntimeException exception) {\n347:         if (exception instanceof TransactionalIdAuthorizationException ||\n348:                         exception instanceof ClusterAuthorizationException) {\n349:             transactionManager.failPendingRequests(new AuthenticationException(exception));\n350:             maybeAbortBatches(exception);\n351:             transactionManager.transitionToUninitialized(exception);\n352:             return true;\n353:         }\n354:         return false;\n355:     }\n356: \n357:     private long sendProducerData(long now) {\n358:         MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot = metadata.fetchMetadataSnapshot();\n359:         // get the list of partitions with data ready to send\n360:         RecordAccumulator.ReadyCheckResult result = this.accumulator.ready(metadataSnapshot, now);\n361: \n362:         // if there are any partitions whose leaders are not known yet, force metadata update\n363:         if (!result.unknownLeaderTopics.isEmpty()) {\n364:             // The set of topics with unknown leader contains topics with leader election pending as well as\n365:             // topics which may have expired. Add the topic again to metadata to ensure it is included\n366:             // and request metadata update, since there are messages to send to the topic.\n367:             for (String topic : result.unknownLeaderTopics)\n368:                 this.metadata.add(topic, now);\n369: \n370:             log.debug(\"Requesting metadata update due to unknown leader topics from the batched records: {}\",\n371:                 result.unknownLeaderTopics);\n372:             this.metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n373:         }\n374: \n375:         // remove any nodes we aren't ready to send to\n376:         Iterator<Node> iter = result.readyNodes.iterator();\n377:         long notReadyTimeout = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n378:         while (iter.hasNext()) {\n379:             Node node = iter.next();\n380:             if (!this.client.ready(node, now)) {\n381:                 // Update just the readyTimeMs of the latency stats, so that it moves forward\n382:                 // every time the batch is ready (then the difference between readyTimeMs and\n383:                 // drainTimeMs would represent how long data is waiting for the node).\n384:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, false);\n385:                 iter.remove();\n386:                 notReadyTimeout = Math.min(notReadyTimeout, this.client.pollDelayMs(node, now));\n387:             } else {\n388:                 // Update both readyTimeMs and drainTimeMs, this would \"reset\" the node\n389:                 // latency.\n390:                 this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, true);\n391:             }\n392:         }\n393: \n394:         // create produce requests\n395:         Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches = this.accumulator.drain(metadataSnapshot, result.readyNodes, this.maxRequestSize, now);\n396:         addToInflightBatches(batches);\n397:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder) {\n398:             // Mute all the partitions drained\n399:             for (List<ProducerBatch> batchList : batches.values()) {\n400:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batchList)\n401:                     this.accumulator.mutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n402:             }\n403:         }\n404: \n405:         accumulator.resetNextBatchExpiryTime();\n406:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);\n407:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);\n408:         expiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\n409: \n410:         // Reset the producer id if an expired batch has previously been sent to the broker. Also update the metrics\n411:         // for expired batches. see the documentation of @TransactionState.resetIdempotentProducerId to understand why\n412:         // we need to reset the producer id here.\n413:         if (!expiredBatches.isEmpty())\n414:             log.trace(\"Expired {} batches in accumulator\", expiredBatches.size());\n415:         for (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\n416:             String errorMessage = \"Expiring \" + expiredBatch.recordCount + \" record(s) for \" + expiredBatch.topicPartition\n417:                 + \":\" + (now - expiredBatch.createdMs) + \" ms has passed since batch creation\";\n418:             failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\n419:             if (transactionManager != null && expiredBatch.inRetry()) {\n420:                 // This ensures that no new batches are drained until the current in flight batches are fully resolved.\n421:                 transactionManager.markSequenceUnresolved(expiredBatch);\n422:             }\n423:         }\n424:         sensors.updateProduceRequestMetrics(batches);\n425: \n426:         // If we have any nodes that are ready to send + have sendable data, poll with 0 timeout so this can immediately\n427:         // loop and try sending more data. Otherwise, the timeout will be the smaller value between next batch expiry\n428:         // time, and the delay time for checking data availability. Note that the nodes may have data that isn't yet\n429:         // sendable due to lingering, backing off, etc. This specifically does not include nodes with sendable data\n430:         // that aren't ready to send since they would cause busy looping.\n431:         long pollTimeout = Math.min(result.nextReadyCheckDelayMs, notReadyTimeout);\n432:         pollTimeout = Math.min(pollTimeout, this.accumulator.nextExpiryTimeMs() - now);\n433:         pollTimeout = Math.max(pollTimeout, 0);\n434:         if (!result.readyNodes.isEmpty()) {\n435:             log.trace(\"Nodes with data ready to send: {}\", result.readyNodes);\n436:             // if some partitions are already ready to be sent, the select time would be 0;\n437:             // otherwise if some partition already has some data accumulated but not ready yet,\n438:             // the select time will be the time difference between now and its linger expiry time;\n439:             // otherwise the select time will be the time difference between now and the metadata expiry time;\n440:             pollTimeout = 0;\n441:         }\n442:         sendProduceRequests(batches, now);\n443:         return pollTimeout;\n444:     }\n445: \n446:     /**\n447:      * Returns true if a transactional request is sent or polled, or if a FindCoordinator request is enqueued\n448:      */\n449:     private boolean maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest() {\n450:         if (transactionManager.hasInFlightRequest()) {\n451:             // as long as there are outstanding transactional requests, we simply wait for them to return\n452:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n453:             return true;\n454:         }\n455: \n456:         if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError()) {\n457:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(transactionManager.lastError());\n458:         } else if (transactionManager.isAborting()) {\n459:             accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(new TransactionAbortedException());\n460:         }\n461: \n462:         TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler = transactionManager.nextRequest(accumulator.hasIncomplete());\n463:         if (nextRequestHandler == null)\n464:             return false;\n465: \n466:         AbstractRequest.Builder<?> requestBuilder = nextRequestHandler.requestBuilder();\n467:         Node targetNode = null;\n468:         try {\n469:             FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType = nextRequestHandler.coordinatorType();\n470:             targetNode = coordinatorType != null ?\n471:                     transactionManager.coordinator(coordinatorType) :\n472:                     client.leastLoadedNode(time.milliseconds()).node();\n473:             if (targetNode != null) {\n474:                 if (!awaitNodeReady(targetNode, coordinatorType)) {\n475:                     log.trace(\"Target node {} not ready within request timeout, will retry when node is ready.\", targetNode);\n476:                     maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n477:                     return true;\n478:                 }\n479:             } else if (coordinatorType != null) {\n480:                 log.trace(\"Coordinator not known for {}, will retry {} after finding coordinator.\", coordinatorType, requestBuilder.apiKey());\n481:                 maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n482:                 return true;\n483:             } else {\n484:                 log.trace(\"No nodes available to send requests, will poll and retry when until a node is ready.\");\n485:                 transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n486:                 client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n487:                 return true;\n488:             }\n489: \n490:             if (nextRequestHandler.isRetry())\n491:                 time.sleep(nextRequestHandler.retryBackoffMs());\n492: \n493:             long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n494:             ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(targetNode.idString(), requestBuilder, currentTimeMs,\n495:                 true, requestTimeoutMs, nextRequestHandler);\n496:             log.debug(\"Sending transactional request {} to node {} with correlation ID {}\", requestBuilder, targetNode, clientRequest.correlationId());\n497:             client.send(clientRequest, currentTimeMs);\n498:             transactionManager.setInFlightCorrelationId(clientRequest.correlationId());\n499:             client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n500:             return true;\n501:         } catch (IOException e) {\n502:             log.debug(\"Disconnect from {} while trying to send request {}. Going \" +\n503:                     \"to back off and retry.\", targetNode, requestBuilder, e);\n504:             // We break here so that we pick up the FindCoordinator request immediately.\n505:             maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n506:             return true;\n507:         }\n508:     }\n509: \n510:     private void maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler) {\n511:         if (nextRequestHandler.needsCoordinator()) {\n512:             transactionManager.lookupCoordinator(nextRequestHandler);\n513:         } else {\n514:             // For non-coordinator requests, sleep here to prevent a tight loop when no node is available\n515:             time.sleep(retryBackoffMs);\n516:             metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n517:         }\n518: \n519:         transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n520:     }\n521: \n522:     private void maybeAbortBatches(RuntimeException exception) {\n523:         if (accumulator.hasIncomplete()) {\n524:             log.error(\"Aborting producer batches due to fatal error\", exception);\n525:             accumulator.abortBatches(exception);\n526:         }\n527:     }\n528: \n529:     /**\n530:      * Start closing the sender (won't actually complete until all data is sent out)\n531:      */\n532:     public void initiateClose() {\n533:         // Ensure accumulator is closed first to guarantee that no more appends are accepted after\n534:         // breaking from the sender loop. Otherwise, we may miss some callbacks when shutting down.\n535:         this.accumulator.close();\n536:         this.running = false;\n537:         this.wakeup();\n538:     }\n539: \n540:     /**\n541:      * Closes the sender without sending out any pending messages.\n542:      */\n543:     public void forceClose() {\n544:         this.forceClose = true;\n545:         initiateClose();\n546:     }\n547: \n548:     public boolean isRunning() {\n549:         return running;\n550:     }\n551: \n552:     private boolean awaitNodeReady(Node node, FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType) throws IOException {\n553:         if (NetworkClientUtils.awaitReady(client, node, time, requestTimeoutMs)) {\n554:             if (coordinatorType == FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType.TRANSACTION) {\n555:                 // Indicate to the transaction manager that the coordinator is ready, allowing it to check ApiVersions\n556:                 // This allows us to bump transactional epochs even if the coordinator is temporarily unavailable at\n557:                 // the time when the abortable error is handled\n558:                 transactionManager.handleCoordinatorReady();\n559:             }\n560:             return true;\n561:         }\n562:         return false;\n563:     }\n564: \n565:     /**\n566:      * Handle a produce response\n567:      */\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames, long now) {\n569:         RequestHeader requestHeader = response.requestHeader();\n570:         int correlationId = requestHeader.correlationId();\n571:         if (response.wasTimedOut()) {\n572:             log.trace(\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\",\n573:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\n574:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n575:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.REQUEST_TIMED_OUT, String.format(\"Disconnected from node %s due to timeout\", response.destination())),\n576:                         correlationId, now, null);\n577:         } else if (response.wasDisconnected()) {\n578:             log.trace(\"Cancelled request with header {} due to node {} being disconnected\",\n579:                 requestHeader, response.destination());\n580:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n581:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NETWORK_EXCEPTION, String.format(\"Disconnected from node %s\", response.destination())),\n582:                         correlationId, now, null);\n583:         } else if (response.versionMismatch() != null) {\n584:             log.warn(\"Cancelled request {} due to a version mismatch with node {}\",\n585:                     response, response.destination(), response.versionMismatch());\n586:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n587:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION), correlationId, now, null);\n588:         } else {\n589:             log.trace(\"Received produce response from node {} with correlation id {}\", response.destination(), correlationId);\n590:             // if we have a response, parse it\n591:             if (response.hasResponse()) {\n592:                 // Sender should exercise PartitionProduceResponse rather than ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse\n593:                 // https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-10696\n594:                 ProduceResponse produceResponse = (ProduceResponse) response.responseBody();\n595:                 // This will be set by completeBatch.\n596:                 Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo = new HashMap<>();\n597:                 produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\n598:                     ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\n600:                             p.baseOffset(),\n601:                             p.logAppendTimeMs(),\n602:                             p.logStartOffset(),\n603:                             p.recordErrors()\n604:                                 .stream()\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\n606:                                 .collect(Collectors.toList()),\n607:                             p.errorMessage(),\n608:                             p.currentLeader());\n609: \n610:                     // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\n611:                     // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\n612:                     // topic name in the response will be empty.\n613:                     // For older versions, topic id is zero, and we will find the batch based on the topic name.\n614:                     TopicPartition tp = (!r.topicId().equals(Uuid.ZERO_UUID) && topicNames.containsKey(r.topicId())) ?\n615:                             new TopicPartition(topicNames.get(r.topicId()), p.index()) :\n616:                             new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\n617: \n618:                     ProducerBatch batch = batches.get(tp);\n619:                     if (batch == null) {\n620:                         throw new IllegalStateException(\"Can't find batch created for topic id \" + r.topicId() +\n621:                                 \" topic name \" + r.name() + \" partition \" + p.index() + \" using \" + topicNames);\n622:                     }\n623:                     completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\n624:                 }));\n625: \n626:                 if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\n630:                         .collect(\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\n633:                     if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\n634:                         updatedPartitions.forEach(\n635:                             part -> log.debug(\"For {} leader was updated.\", part)\n636:                         );\n637:                     }\n638:                 }\n639: \n640:                 this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\n641:             } else {\n642:                 // this is the acks = 0 case, just complete all requests\n643:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values()) {\n644:                     completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NONE), correlationId, now, null);\n645:                 }\n646:             }\n647:         }\n648:     }\n649: \n650:     /**\n651:      * Complete or retry the given batch of records.\n652:      *\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\n654:      * @param response The produce response\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\n658:      */\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\n662: \n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\n667:             log.warn(\n668:                 \"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n669:                 correlationId,\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\n680:                 log.warn(\n681:                     \"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n682:                     correlationId,\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\n691:                 //\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\n694:             } else {\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\n699:             }\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\n702:                     log.warn(\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \" +\n703:                             \"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\",\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\n705:                 } else {\n706:                     log.warn(\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \" +\n707:                             \"to request metadata update now\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\n708:                 }\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\n710:                     log.debug(\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\n715:                     }\n716:                 }\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n718:             }\n719:         } else {\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\n721:         }\n722: \n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n726:     }\n727: \n728:     /**\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\n730:      * e.g \"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\"\n731:      */\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\n734:                 \"\" : String.format(\".             // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\n776: There are some paths that we don't try to find the OffsetOfMaxTimestamp\\n254:      * to avoid expensive records iteration. Those paths include follower append and index recovery. In order to\\n255:      * avoid inconsistent time index, we let all paths find shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp instead of OffsetOfMaxTimestamp.\\n256:      * <p>\\n257:      * Let's define the shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp: It is last offset of the batch having max timestamp. If there are\\n258:      * many batches having same max timestamp, we pick up the earliest batch.\\n259:      * <p>\\n260:      * There are five cases of finding shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp to return:\\n261:      * 1) version 0: It is always the -1\\n262:      * 2) LogAppendTime with single batch: It is the offset of last record\\n263:      * 3) LogAppendTime with many single-record batches: Those single-record batches have same max timestamp, so we return\\n264:      *                                                   the base offset, which is equal to the last offset of earliest batch\\n265:      * 4) CreateTime with single batch: We return offset of last record to follow the spec we mentioned above. Of course,\\n266:      *                                  we do have the OffsetOfMaxTimestamp for this case, but we want to make all paths\\n267:      *                                  find the New batches are drained at line 395\n3. They're added to inFlightBatches at line 396\n4. Some in-flight batches from previous iterations are found to be expired (line 406-407)\n5. Produce requests for the newly drained batches get queued at line 442, and their buffers might be reallocated from the same pool\n8. When client.poll() executes at line 340, it serializes these requests and reads from the MemoryRecords buffer\n9. Now I understand the flow better. When a batch response is received, `handleProduceResponse()` is called, which calls `completeBatch()`, which calls `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch()` at line 750 to deallocate the batch.\n\nNow let me think about the actual race condition. Looking at the code in sendProducerData():\n\n```java\nList<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);  // line 406\nList<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);   // line 407\nexpiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);                              // line 408\n\n// ...\n\nfor (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {                         // line 415\n    // ...\n    failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);     // line 418\n    // ...\n}\n\n// ...\n\nsendProduceRequests(batches, now);                                          // line 442\n```\n\nThe issue is:\n1. A batch is in the `inFlightBatches` map (meaning a request was already sent for it)\n2. The batch is still being serialized/sent to the network by the KafkaClient\n3. However, at line 406, `getExpiredInflightBatches()` returns this batch as expired\n4. At line 418, `failBatch()` is called, which calls `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch()` at line 835\n5. `maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch()` calls `this.accumulator.deallocate(batch)` at line 174\n6. `deallocate()` returns the buffer to the pool at line 1032\n7. The pool can immediately reuse this buffer for a new batch\n\n\n8. Meanwhile, the KafkaClient is still serializing/sending the original batch's request, which tries to read from the now-reused buffer!\n\nThe critical timing here is that `client.send()` at line 914 only queues the request—actual serialization happens later in `client.poll()` after `sendProducerData()` returns at line 340. This means the buffer deallocation can occur before the serialization even begins.\n\nThe sequence unfolds like this: batches get drained and queued with `client.send()`, then expired batches from prior iterations are found and deallocated, `sendProducerData()` completes, and finally `client.poll()` serializes all queued requests. If a batch's buffer was reused between queueing and serialization, the request would try to read from corrupted memory.\n\nThough actually, I need to reconsider whether step 3 and step 4 can even affect the same batch here.\n\nAt line 406, `getExpiredInflightBatches()` retrieves batches from `inFlightBatches` that have exceeded the delivery timeout. Since we just added new batches at line 396, could one of those immediately expire? Looking at the `hasReachedDeliveryTimeout()` check, a freshly created batch shouldn't have reached the timeout yet, so it wouldn't appear in the expired list. Looking back at line 395:```java\nMap<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches = this.accumulator.drain(metadataSnapshot, result.readyNodes, this.maxRequestSize, now);\n```\n\nThis `drain()` method returns batches that are ready to send. These batches may have been created in PREVIOUS iterations of sendProducerData()! They were waiting in the accumulator's queues for the right moment to be sent.\n\nThen at line 406, `getExpiredInflightBatches()` returns batches from `inFlightBatches` that have timed out. These are batches that were sent in PREVIOUS iterations and are still waiting for responses.\n\nSo the race condition could be:1. In iteration N-1, batches A and B are sent (added to inFlightBatches)\n2. In iteration N, batches A and B are still in inFlightBatches\n3. But batches A and B have now timed out (reached delivery timeout)\n4. So at line 406, they're found as expired\n5. At line 418, they're failed and deallocated, returning their buffers to the pool\n6. But what if batches A and B's requests are STILL BEING SENT to the network?\n\nActually, looking at line 180-200 again, when a batch is found to be expired in getExpiredInflightBatches(), it's REMOVED from the inFlightBatches map (line 191: `iter.remove()`). So it's no longer tracked as in-flight.\n\n\nThe critical question is whether the batch's request has already been serialized and sent to the network by the time it's marked as expired. The sequence is: batch gets added to inFlightBatches, then queued with client.send(), then sendProducerData() returns. The actual network transmission happens later when client.poll() is called, which is where the request gets serialized and sent. A response eventually comes back and triggers handleProduceResponse() to remove the batch from inFlightBatches.\n\nThe vulnerability exists in the window between when client.send() queues the request and when client.poll() actually serializes it to the socket. If the batch expires and gets deallocated during this gap, its buffer could be reused while the serialization is still reading from it, corrupting the data being sent.\n\nThe batch's buffer is captured when MemoryRecords.build() is called at line 874, creating a reference that gets embedded through ProduceRequestData into the ProduceRequest and ultimately the ClientRequest.
